Key examples:\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/kubelet/pkg/cri/streaming/errors.go:NewErrorTooManyInFlight()` creates `status.Error(codes.ResourceExhausted, ...)`\\n- `test/e2e/storage/drivers/csi-test/mock/service/node.go` uses `status.Error(codes.NotFound, ...)` and `status.Error(codes.Internal, ...)`\\n- Generated service code in `staging/src/k8s.io/kms/apis/v2/api_grpc.pb.go` returns `status.Errorf(codes.Unimplemented, ...)`\\n\\n**HTTP Translation Pattern:**\\nThe translation from gRPC to HTTP uses a switch statement mapping gRPC codes to HTTP status codes:\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/kubelet/pkg/cri/streaming/errors.go:WriteError()` - Core translation function:\\n  - `codes.NotFound` → `http.StatusNotFound`\\n  - `codes.ResourceExhausted` → `http.StatusTooManyRequests`\\n  - Default → `http.StatusInternalServerError`\\n\\n- `vendor/github.com/grpc-ecosystem/grpc-gateway/v2/runtime/errors.go:HTTPStatusFromCode()` - Comprehensive mapping:\\n  - `codes.OK` → `200`\\n  - `codes.InvalidArgument` → `400`\\n  - `codes.DeadlineExceeded` → `504`\\n  - `codes.NotFound` → `404`\\n  - `codes.PermissionDenied` → `403`\\n  - `codes.Unauthenticated` → `401`\\n\\n**Error Propagation Chain:**\\n- Service implementations return gRPC status errors\\n- `pkg/volume/util/metrics.go:getErrorCode()` extracts status codes for metrics\\n- `pkg/probe/grpc/grpc.go:Probe()` handles codes like `codes.Unimplemented` and `codes.DeadlineExceeded`\\n- HTTP handlers use `WriteError()` to translate before responding\\n\\n### etcd-io/etcd\\n\\n**Error Creation Pattern:**\\netcd uses pre-defined gRPC error variables with specific codes, centralized in `api/v3rpc/rpctypes/error.go`:\\n- Server-side errors defined with status codes:\\n  - `ErrGRPCEmptyKey = status.Error(codes.InvalidArgument, ...)`\\n  - `ErrGRPCLeaseNotFound = status.Error(codes.NotFound, ...)`\\n  - `ErrGRPCMemberExist = status.Error(codes.FailedPrecondition, ...)`\\n  - `ErrGRPCNoLeader = status.Error(codes.Unavailable, ...)`\\n  - `ErrGRPCInvalidAuthToken = status.Error(codes.Unauthenticated, ...)`\\n  - `ErrGRPCPermissionDenied = status.Error(codes.PermissionDenied, ...)`\\n  - `ErrGRPCCorrupt = status.Error(codes.DataLoss, ...)`\\n\\n**HTTP Translation Pattern:**\\netcd uses `toGRPCErrorMap` to translate internal errors to gRPC errors in `server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/util.go:togRPCError()`:\\n- Maps domain errors (e.g., `membership.ErrIDNotFound`) to gRPC status errors\\n- Falls back to `status.Error(codes.Unknown, ...)` for unmapped errors\\n- Handles context errors specially: `context.Canceled` and `context.DeadlineExceeded` are passed through\\n\\nHTTP responses are handled in `server/etcdserver/api/etcdhttp/peer.go`:\\n- `membership.ErrIDNotFound` → `http.StatusNotFound`\\n- `membership.ErrMemberNotLearner` → `http.StatusPreconditionFailed`\\n- `errors.ErrLearnerNotReady` → `http.StatusPreconditionFailed`\\n\\n**Error Propagation Chain:**\\n1. Business logic in etcdserver generates domain errors\\n2. `server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/util.go:togRPCError()` converts to gRPC status errors\\n3. `server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/interceptor.go` - unary and stream interceptors enforce capabilities and return errors\\n4. `client/v3/retry_interceptor.go:contextErrToGRPCErr()` - client-side handler converts context errors to gRPC status\\n5. etcd-io/etcd, and grafana/grafana.\\n\\n### Kubernetes (kubernetes/kubernetes)\\n\\n**Error Creation Pattern:**\\nKubernetes creates gRPC errors at service boundaries. Key examples:\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/kubelet/pkg/cri/streaming/errors.go:NewErrorTooManyInFlight()` creates `status.Error(codes.ResourceExhausted, ...)`\\n- `test/e2e/storage/drivers/csi-test/mock/service/node.go` uses `status.Error(codes.NotFound, ...)` and `status.Error(codes.Internal, ...)`\\n- Generated service code in `staging/src/k8s.io/kms/apis/v2/api_grpc.pb.go` returns `status.Errorf(codes.Unimplemented, ...)`\\n\\n**HTTP Translation Pattern:**\\nThe translation from gRPC to HTTP uses a switch statement mapping gRPC codes to HTTP status codes:\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/kubelet/pkg/cri/streaming/errors.go:WriteError()` - Core translation function:\\n  - `codes.NotFound` → `http.StatusNotFound`\\n  - `codes.ResourceExhausted` → `http.StatusTooManyRequests`\\n  - Default → `http.StatusInternalServerError`\\n\\n- `vendor/github.com/grpc-ecosystem/grpc-gateway/v2/runtime/errors.go:HTTPStatusFromCode()` - Comprehensive mapping:\\n  - `codes.OK` → `200`\\n  - `codes.InvalidArgument` → `400`\\n  - `codes.DeadlineExceeded` → `504`\\n  - `codes.NotFound` → `404`\\n  - `codes.PermissionDenied` → `403`\\n  - `codes.Unauthenticated` → `401`\\n\\n**Error Propagation Chain:**\\n- Service implementations return gRPC status errors\\n- `pkg/volume/util/metrics.go:getErrorCode()` extracts status codes for metrics\\n- `pkg/probe/grpc/grpc.go:Probe()` handles codes like `codes.Unimplemented` and `codes.DeadlineExceeded`\\n- HTTP handlers use `WriteError()` to translate before responding\\n\\n### etcd-io/etcd\\n\\n**Error Creation Pattern:**\\netcd uses pre-defined gRPC error variables with specific codes, centralized in `api/v3rpc/rpctypes/error.go`:\\n- Server-side errors defined with status codes:\\n  - `ErrGRPCEmptyKey = status.Error(codes.InvalidArgument, ...)`\\n  - `ErrGRPCLeaseNotFound = status.Error(codes.NotFound, ...)`\\n  - `ErrGRPCMemberExist = status.Error(codes.FailedPrecondition, ...)`\\n  - `ErrGRPCNoLeader = status.Error(codes.Unavailable, ...)`\\n  - `ErrGRPCInvalidAuthToken = status.Error(codes.Unauthenticated, ...)`\\n  - `ErrGRPCPermissionDenied = status.Error(codes.PermissionDenied, ...)`\\n  - `ErrGRPCCorrupt = status.Error(codes.DataLoss, ...)`\\n\\n**HTTP Translation Pattern:**\\netcd uses `toGRPCErrorMap` to translate internal errors to gRPC errors in `server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/util.go:togRPCError()`:\\n- Maps domain errors (e.g., `membership.ErrIDNotFound`) to gRPC status errors\\n- Falls back to `status.Error(codes.Unknown, ...)` for unmapped errors\\n- Handles context errors specially: `context.Canceled` and `context.DeadlineExceeded` are passed through\\n\\nHTTP responses are handled in `server/etcdserver/api/etcdhttp/peer.go`:\\n- `membership.ErrIDNotFound` → `http.StatusNotFound`\\n- `membership.ErrMemberNotLearner` → `http.StatusPreconditionFailed`\\n- `errors.ErrLearnerNotReady` → `http.StatusPreconditionFailed`\\n\\n**Error Propagation Chain:**\\n1. Business logic in etcdserver generates domain errors\\n2. `server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/util.go:togRPCError()` converts to gRPC status errors\\n3. `server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/interceptor.go` - unary and stream interceptors enforce capabilities and return errors\\n4. `client/v3/retry_interceptor.go:contextErrToGRPCErr()` - client-side handler converts context errors to gRPC status\\n5. HTTP handlers in `peer.go` translate to HTTP status codes\\n\\n### Grafana (grafana/grafana)\\n\\n**Error Creation Pattern:**\\nGrafana creates gRPC errors at service boundaries:\\n- `pkg/services/authz/rbac/service.go:ListPermission()` - `status.Error(codes.NotFound, \\\"unsupported resource\\\")`\\n- Service implementation returns gRPC status errors directly\\n\\n**HTTP Translation Pattern:**\\nGrafana uses grpc-gateway middleware to convert gRPC errors:\\n- `pkg/services/authz/zanzana/server/openfga_server.go:NewOpenFGAHttpServer()` uses:\\n  - `runtime.WithErrorHandler()` - Custom HTTP error handler\\n  - `runtime.WithStreamErrorHandler()` - Stream error handler\\n  - Calls `serverErrors.ConvertToEncodedErrorCode(status.Convert(e))` to convert gRPC status\\n  - Calls `httpmiddleware.CustomHTTPErrorHandler()` to write HTTP response\\n\\n- `pkg/storage/unified/resource/errors.go:HTTPStatusFromCode()` - Maps gRPC codes to HTTP:\\n  - Uses `runtime.HTTPStatusFromCode(st.Code())` for standard mapping\\n  - Falls back to `500` for unmapped codes\\n\\n**Error Propagation Chain:**\\n1. Service methods return gRPC status errors\\n2. `pkg/tsdb/influxdb/fsql/fsql.go:Query()` - Receives gRPC errors from FlightSQL client\\n3. Checks `status.FromError(err)` and switches on `grpcStatusErr.Code()`:\\n   - `codes.InvalidArgument` → `backend.StatusBadRequest`\\n   - `codes.PermissionDenied` → `backend.StatusForbidden`\\n   - `codes.NotFound` → `backend.StatusNotFound`\\n   - `codes.Unavailable` → `http.StatusServiceUnavailable`\\n   - `codes.Unauthenticated` → `backend.StatusUnauthorized`\\n   - Default → `backend.StatusInternal`\\n4. grpc-gateway middleware translates to HTTP before returning to client\\n5. `pkg/plugins/manager/client/client.go` - Handles `codes.Canceled` for request cancellation\\n6. `pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/client_v2.go:handleGrpcStatusError()` - Error source handling\\n\\n### Key Patterns and Differences\\n\\n**Centralized vs Distributed Error Creation:**\\n- **etcd**: Centralized in `rpctypes/error.go` - all gRPC errors defined once\\n- **Kubernetes**: Distributed at call sites - errors created where needed\\n- **Grafana**: Mix - some pre-defined, some created at call sites\\n\\n**Error Mapping Strategies:**\\n- **etcd**: Explicit `toGRPCErrorMap` for domain-to-gRPC conversion\\n- **Kubernetes**: Use grpc-gateway's built-in HTTP status mapping\\n- **Grafana**: Custom middleware with `status.Convert()` and error handler callbacks\\n\\n**Propagation Mechanisms:**\\n- **etcd**: Context errors flow through interceptors unchanged; handled separately\\n- **Kubernetes**: Direct mapping at HTTP boundaries via `WriteError()`\\n- **Grafana**: grpc-gateway middleware abstracts the translation\\n\\n**Code Organization:**\\n- **etcd**: Clear separation in `rpctypes/error.go` (creation) and `v3rpc/util.go` (translation)\\n- **Kubernetes**: Vendored grpc-gateway handles translation; service code creates errors\\n- **Grafana**: Service code creates errors; gateway middleware handles translation\"\n   248→}\n   249→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. Core translation function:\\n  - `codes.NotFound` → `http.StatusNotFound`\\n  - `codes.ResourceExhausted` → `http.StatusTooManyRequests`\\n  - Default → `http.StatusInternalServerError`\\n\\n- `vendor/github.com/grpc-ecosystem/grpc-gateway/v2/runtime/errors.go:HTTPStatusFromCode()` - `ErrGRPCCorrupt = status.Error(codes.DataLoss, ...)`\\n\\n**HTTP Translation Pattern:**\\netcd uses `toGRPCErrorMap` to translate internal errors to gRPC errors in `server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/util.go:togRPCError()`:\\n- Maps domain errors (e.g., `membership.ErrIDNotFound`) to gRPC status errors\\n- Falls back to `status.Error(codes.Unknown, ...)` for unmapped errors\\n- Handles context errors specially: `context.Canceled` and `context.DeadlineExceeded` are passed through\\n\\nHTTP responses are handled in `server/etcdserver/api/etcdhttp/peer.go`:\\n- `membership.ErrIDNotFound` → `http.StatusNotFound`\\n- `membership.ErrMemberNotLearner` → `http.StatusPreconditionFailed`\\n- `errors.ErrLearnerNotReady` → `http.StatusPreconditionFailed`\\n\\n**Error Propagation Chain:**\\n1. Business logic in etcdserver generates domain errors\\n2. `server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/util.go:togRPCError()` converts to gRPC status errors\\n3. `server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/interceptor.go` - unary and stream interceptors enforce capabilities and return errors\\n4. `client/v3/retry_interceptor.go:contextErrToGRPCErr()` - client-side handler converts context errors to gRPC status\\n5. HTTP handlers in `peer.go` translate to HTTP status codes\\n\\n### Grafana (grafana/grafana)\\n\\n**Error Creation Pattern:**\\nGrafana creates gRPC errors at service boundaries:\\n- `pkg/services/authz/rbac/service.go:ListPermission()` - `status.Error(codes.NotFound, \\\"unsupported resource\\\")`\\n- Service implementation returns gRPC status errors directly\\n\\n**HTTP Translation Pattern:**\\nGrafana uses grpc-gateway middleware to convert gRPC errors:\\n- `pkg/services/authz/zanzana/server/openfga_server.go:NewOpenFGAHttpServer()` uses:\\n  - `runtime.WithErrorHandler()` - Custom HTTP error handler\\n  - `runtime.WithStreamErrorHandler()` - Stream error handler\\n  - Calls `serverErrors.ConvertToEncodedErrorCode(status.Convert(e))` to convert gRPC status\\n  - Calls `httpmiddleware.CustomHTTPErrorHandler()` to write HTTP response\\n\\n- `pkg/storage/unified/resource/errors.go:HTTPStatusFromCode()` - Maps gRPC codes to HTTP:\\n  - Uses `runtime.HTTPStatusFromCode(st.Code())` for standard mapping\\n  - Falls back to `500` for unmapped codes\\n\\n**Error Propagation Chain:**\\n1. Service methods return gRPC status errors\\n2. `pkg/tsdb/influxdb/fsql/fsql.go:Query()` - Receives gRPC errors from FlightSQL client\\n3. Checks `status.FromError(err)` and switches on `grpcStatusErr.Code()`:\\n   - `codes.InvalidArgument` → `backend.StatusBadRequest`\\n   - `codes.PermissionDenied` → `backend.StatusForbidden`\\n   - `codes.NotFound` → `backend.StatusNotFound`\\n   - `codes.Unavailable` → `http.StatusServiceUnavailable`\\n   - `codes.Unauthenticated` → `backend.StatusUnauthorized`\\n   - Default → `backend.StatusInternal`\\n4. grpc-gateway middleware translates to HTTP before returning to client\\n5. `pkg/plugins/manager/client/client.go` - Handles `codes.Canceled` for request cancellation\\n6. `pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/client_v2.go:handleGrpcStatusError()` - Error source handling\\n\\n### Key Patterns and Differences\\n\\n**Centralized vs Distributed Error Creation:**\\n- **etcd**: Centralized in `rpctypes/error.go` - all gRPC errors defined once\\n- **Kubernetes**: Distributed at call sites - errors created where needed\\n- **Grafana**: Mix - some pre-defined, some created at call sites\\n\\n**Error Mapping Strategies:**\\n- **etcd**: Explicit `toGRPCErrorMap` for domain-to-gRPC conversion\\n- **Kubernetes**: Use grpc-gateway's built-in HTTP status mapping\\n- **Grafana**: Custom middleware with `status.Convert()` and error handler callbacks\\n\\n**Propagation Mechanisms:**\\n- **etcd**: Context errors flow through interceptors unchanged; handled separately\\n- **Kubernetes**: Direct mapping at HTTP boundaries via `WriteError()`\\n- **Grafana**: grpc-gateway middleware abstracts the translation\\n\\n**Code Organization:**\\n- **etcd**: Clear separation in `rpctypes/error.go` (creation) and `v3rpc/util.go` (translation)\\n- **Kubernetes**: Vendored grpc-gateway handles translation; service code creates errors\\n- **Grafana**: Service code creates errors; gateway middleware handles translation\"\n}\n","numLines":249,"startLine":1,"totalLines":249}}}
